#  Amazon.com Gift Card Balance Reload 
[ 4.7  _4.7 out of 5 stars_ ](javascript:void\(0\)) [ 531,290 ratings ](https://www.amazon.com/dp/B0CHTVMXZJ#averageCustomerReviewsAnchor)
##  Add funds directly to your Amazon Gift Card balance 
Amazon's Choice highlights highly rated, well-priced products available to ship immediately. 
Amazon's Choice 
Brief content visible, double tap to read full content.
Full content visible, double tap to read brief content.
Reload type:  One Time Reload 
Make a Reload type selection 
  * One Time Reload 
  * Low Balance Auto-Reload 
  * Scheduled Auto-Reload 


Reload amount:  $25.00 
  * $25 
  * $50 
  * $100 
  * $


  * Add funds to your Amazon gift card balance, then use your balance to manage how much you spend while shopping. 
  * Set up Auto-Reload to automatically reload your gift card balance on a particular date, week, month or when your balance gets low (below a certain amount). 
  * Save up for a purchase by adding funds to your gift card balance. 
  * Checkout faster when you reload to your gift card balance in advance. 
  * Reloaded funds never expire and have no fees. 
  * Amazon Reload purchases are not refundable or redeemable for cash, except as required by law.

## From the manufacturer
Amazon Reload 
###  * 
With Amazon Reload, you can add funds quickly and easily using your credit, debit, or prepaid gift card and then use your balance toward millions of items on Amazon. 
![Amazon Reload](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
![](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
#  Two easy ways to add funds to your balance 
![Reload](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
#  Reload 
With Reload, you can add funds to your Amazon Gift Card balance with a one-time, manual reload on a date of your choice. 
![Auto-Reload](https://images-na.ssl-images-amazon.com/images/G/01/x-locale/common/grey-pixel.gif)
#  Auto-Reload 
Want to set it and forget it? You can set up Auto-Reload to schedule automated fund transfers to your balance--either when your funds drop below a certain amount or on a regularly scheduled daily, weekly, or monthly basis. 
  * ### 
How does it work? 
Each reload transaction adds an Amazon Gift Card to your Amazon Gift Card balance. 
  * ### 
Are there any maintenance fees for the funds I reload and does the balance I reload expire? 
No. Amazon Does not charge any fees for you balance and there is no expiration date for the balance you reload. 
  * ### 
What can I use my balance to shop for? 
You can use your balance toward eligible items on Amazon, including physical products, digital content, and offers from third party merchants. 
  * ### 
Can I change my Auto-Reload setting? 
Yes. Go to the Your Account View Gift Card balance page to change the amount of the Auto-Reload, the amount to trigger the Auto-Reload, or to turn off Auto-Reload.

[How customer reviews and ratings work](javascript:void\(0\))
Customer Reviews, including Product Star Ratings help customers to learn more about the product and decide whether it is the right product for them.
To calculate the overall star rating and percentage breakdown by star, we don’t use a simple average. Instead, our system considers things like how recent a review is and if the reviewer bought the item on Amazon. It also analyzed reviews to verify trustworthiness.
[Learn more how customers reviews work on Amazon](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_omni_lm_btn?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)

### Customers say
Customers find the Amazon gift card easy to use and appreciate its functionality, with funds appearing almost instantly in their accounts. They value its convenience for gift-giving, particularly for birthdays and holidays, and consider it a smart way to manage spending with no fees or second guessing. The card is particularly useful for managing budgets and adding funds, with one customer noting it works well for consolidating Visa gift cards.

##### [ _5.0 out of 5 stars_ NEW ERA OF FLEXIBILITY!! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R1E19O3K62PIVE/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B0CHTKNWBL)
Reviewed in the United States on June 28, 2025
Reload type: One Time Reload[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
Reloading Amazon Gift Cards: A New Era of Flexibility:Reloading an Amazon gift card has always been a convenient way to manage spending on the platform, but the recent shift in how Amazon handles gift card balances has truly elevated the experience.It's now not just about adding funds, but about having unprecedented control over when and how those funds are used, making the whole process significantly more user-friendly.In the past, the moment you redeemed an Amazon gift card, its value was immediately applied to your next purchase, often forcing you to use it even if you had other payment methods preferred for that specific transaction. This used to be frustrating, especially for those who liked to save gift card balances for particular items or for a rainy day.Thankfully, Amazon has listened to customer feedback and implemented a game-changing feature: the ability to hold your gift card balance and use it whenever you choose.This means you can reload your card, see the balance instantly credited to your account, and then decide to use it for a small everyday purchase or save it up for a larger, more significant one.It functions just like any other payment method now, giving you the freedom to prioritize credit card rewards, use a debit card, or dip into your gift card balance as you see fit. The reloading process itself remains as seamless as ever, typically taking just a few minutes for the funds to appear.The real win, however, is this newfound flexibility. It transforms Amazon gift cards from a "use it or lose it" immediate credit to a truly versatile and manageable payment option.This enhanced control over your funds makes reloading Amazon gift cards not just a practical choice, but a genuinely great one

##### [_5.0 out of 5 stars_ Great way to use prepaid refund/rebate debit cards! ](https://www.amazon.com/gp/customer-reviews/R2S12U6MDGA96M/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_ttl?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B0CHTKNWBL)
Reviewed in the United States on June 6, 2025
Reload type: Low Balance Auto-Reload[Verified Purchase](https://www.amazon.com/gp/help/customer/display.html/ref=cm_cr_dp_d_rvw_avp?nodeId=G8UYX7LALQC8V9KA)
Prepaid debit cards are very popular these days, instead of checks, for things like rebates. Except some have fees that pile up, eroding your balance. Or you can't really use it, because it won't fully cover the cost of anything, and many retailers won't accept multiple payment methods. In the very least, you may get stuck with a balance you can never fully use. Or you forget about it completely.As soon as I get one of those prepaid debit cards, I use it to reload my Amazon gift card balance. I get all of the money safely off the card before it can accrue any fees, expire, or be forgotten, and have every penny available to spend across one or more purchases.
